class="ms-2"><p class="flex items-center gap-2 justify-between font-medium text-stone-900 py-1 dark:text-white mb-1 not-first:mt-4">Reference</p><ul><li><a class="py-1 px-2 group rounded-md flex items-center transition-colors relative hover:text-stone-900 dark:hover:text-stone-200" href="/docs/react/reference/faq"><span class="">FAQs</span></a></li><li><a class="py-1 px-2 group rounded-md class="py-1 px-2 group rounded-md flex items-center transition-colors relative hover:text-stone-900 dark:hover:text-stone-200" href="/docs/react/reference/performance"><span class="">Performance tips</span></a></li><li><div class="ms-2"><details class="group not-first:mt-4" open=""><summary class="list-none"><div class="flex items-center gap-2 justify-between font-medium text-stone-900 py-1 dark:text-white mb-1 not-first:mt-4"><span class="flex-1">Design patterns</span><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down rounded-xs text-stone-700 dark:text-stone-100 group-open:rotate-180 transition-transform group-hover:text-stone-500 text-stone-400 dark:text-stone-600" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></div></summary><ul><li><a class="py-1 px-2 group rounded-md flex items-center transition-colors relative hover:text-stone-900 dark:hover:text-stone-200" href="/docs/react/reference/design-patterns/form"><span class="">Forms</span></a></li><li><a class="py-1 px-2 group rounded-md flex items-center transition-colors relative hover:text-stone-900 dark:hover:text-stone-200" href="/docs/react/reference/design-patterns/organization"><span class="">Organization/Team</span></a></li><li><a class="py-1 px-2 group rounded-md flex items-center transition-colors relative hover:text-stone-900 dark:hover:text-stone-200" href="/docs/react/reference/design-patterns/history-patterns"><span class="">History Patterns</span></a></li></ul></details></div></li></ul></div></li></ul><div aria-hidden="true" class="h-12 right-0 sticky bottom-0 left-0 bg-linear-to-t from-white  to-transparent dark:from-stone-950 hidden md:block"></div></div></div></div><div class="md:col-span-8 lg:col-span-9 flex gap-12"><div class="w-full" data-pagefind-body="true" data-pagefind-meta="framework: react"><div class="overflow-hidden pb-8 pt-[calc(61px+2rem)] md:pt-8 md:max-w-3xl mx-auto prose dark:prose-invert dark:prose-code:bg-stone-900"><h1 id="comaps">CoMaps</h1>
<p>CoMaps are key-value objects that work like JavaScript objects. You can access properties with dot notation and define typed fields that provide TypeScript safety. They&#x27;re ideal for structured data that needs type validation.</p>
<h2 id="creating-comaps" class="group"><a href="#creating-comaps" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Creating CoMaps</span></h2>
<p>CoMaps are typically defined with <code>co.map()</code> and specifying primitive fields using <code>z</code> (see <a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/covalues/overview">Defining schemas: CoValues</a> for more details on primitive fields):</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">import</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { co</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> z } </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">from</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "jazz-tools"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  startDate</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  status</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.literal</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">([</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"planning"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "active"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "completed"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">])</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  coordinator</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.optional</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(Member)</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> type</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> co</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">loaded</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">typeof</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> Project>;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> type</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> ProjectInitShape</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> co</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">input</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">typeof</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> Project>; </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// type accepted by `Project.create`</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>You can create either struct-like CoMaps with fixed fields (as above) or record-like CoMaps for key-value pairs:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Inventory</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.record</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.number</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">());</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>To instantiate a CoMap:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Project</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Spring Planting"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  startDate</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> new</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"2025-03-15"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">)</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  status</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "planning"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> inventory</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Inventory</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  tomatoes</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 48</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  basil</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 12</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h3 id="ownership" class="group"><a href="#ownership" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Ownership</span></h3>
<p>When creating CoMaps, you can specify ownership to control access:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Create with default owner (current user)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> privateProject</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Project</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "My Herb Garden"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  startDate</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> new</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"2025-04-01"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">)</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  status</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "planning"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Create with shared ownership</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> gardenGroup</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Group</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">gardenGroup</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.addMember</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(memberAccount</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "writer"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> communityProject</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Project</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Community Vegetable Plot"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    startDate</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> new</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"2025-03-20"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">)</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    status</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "planning"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  { owner</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> gardenGroup }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>See <a href="/docs/react/permissions-and-sharing/overview">Groups as permission scopes</a> for more information on how to use groups to control access to CoMaps.</p>
<h2 id="reading-from-comaps" class="group"><a href="#reading-from-comaps" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Reading from CoMaps</span></h2>
<p>CoMaps can be accessed using familiar JavaScript object notation:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">project</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.name); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// "Spring Planting"</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">project</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.status); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// "planning"</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h3 id="handling-optional-fields" class="group"><a href="#handling-optional-fields" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Handling Optional Fields</span></h3>
<p>Optional fields require checks before access:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">if</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> (</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">project</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.coordinator) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">  console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">project</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">coordinator</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.name); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Safe access</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">}</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h3 id="recursive-references" class="group"><a href="#recursive-references" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Recursive references</span></h3>
<p>You can wrap references in getters. This allows you to defer evaluation until the property is accessed. This technique is particularly useful for defining circular references, including recursive (self-referencing) schemas, or mutually recursive schemas.</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">import</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { co</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> z } </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">from</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "jazz-tools"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  startDate</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  status</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.literal</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">([</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"planning"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "active"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "completed"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">])</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  coordinator</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.optional</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(Member)</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  get</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> subProject</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">() {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">    return</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Project</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.optional</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> type</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> co</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">loaded</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">typeof</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> Project>;</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>When the recursive references involve more complex types, it is sometimes required to specify the getter return type:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="6 7 8" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ProjectWithTypedGetter</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  startDate</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  status</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.literal</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">([</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"planning"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "active"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "completed"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">])</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  coordinator</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.optional</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(Member)</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line diff add"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  get</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> subProjects</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> co</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">Optional</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">co</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">List</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">typeof</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> Project>> {</span></span>
<span class="line diff add"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">    return</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.optional</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.list</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(Project));</span></span>
<span class="line diff add"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> type</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> co</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">loaded</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">typeof</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> Project>;</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h3 id="partial" class="group"><a href="#partial" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Partial</span></h3>
<p>For convenience Jazz provies a dedicated API for making all the properties of a CoMap optional:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  startDate</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  status</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.literal</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">([</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"planning"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "active"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "completed"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">])</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ProjectDraft</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Project</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.partial</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">();</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// The fields are all optional now</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ProjectDraft</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({});</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h3 id="pick" class="group"><a href="#pick" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Pick</span></h3>
<p>You can also pick specific fields from a CoMap:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  startDate</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  status</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.literal</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">([</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"planning"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "active"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "completed"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">])</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ProjectStep1</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Project</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.pick</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> true</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  startDate</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> true</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// We don't provide the status field</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ProjectStep1</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "My project"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  startDate</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> new</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"2025-04-01"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">)</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h3 id="working-with-record-comaps" class="group"><a href="#working-with-record-comaps" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Working with Record CoMaps</span></h3>
<p>For record-type CoMaps, you can access values using bracket notation:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> inventory</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Inventory</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  tomatoes</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 48</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  peppers</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 24</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  basil</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 12</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(inventory[</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"tomatoes"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">]); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// 48</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h2 id="updating-comaps" class="group"><a href="#updating-comaps" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Updating CoMaps</span></h2>
<p>To update a CoMap&#x27;s properties, use the <code>$jazz.set</code> method:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">project</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.set</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"name"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Spring Vegetable Garden"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Update name</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">project</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.set</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"startDate"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> new</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"2025-03-20"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">)); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Update date</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<div class="border-l-4 p-4 pl-6 dark:bg-red-200/5 overflow-hidden relative rounded-sm border-blue-400 bg-blue-50 dark:border-blue-500 dark:bg-blue-200/5 flex gap-2 items-center my-4"><span class="text-sm font-bold flex items-center gap-1 text-blue-700 dark:text-blue-400"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="72" height="72" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-info rounded-lg text-stone-700 dark:text-stone-100 absolute -z-10 right-0 opacity-5 top-0 rotate-12 pointer-events-none" aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-info rounded-xs text-stone-700 dark:text-stone-100" aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg></span><span class="text-sm"><p>The <code>$jazz</code> namespace is available on all CoValues, and provides access to methods to modify and load CoValues,
as well as access common properties like <code>id</code> and <code>owner</code>.</p></span></div>
<p>When updating references to other CoValues, you can provide both the new CoValue or a JSON object from which the new CoValue will be created.</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Dog</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.plainText</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Person</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.plainText</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  dog</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> Dog</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> person</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Person</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "John"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  dog</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Rex"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Update the dog field using a CoValue</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">person</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.set</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"dog"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Dog</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({ name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.plainText</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"Fido"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">) }));</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Or use a plain JSON object</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">person</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.set</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"dog"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Fido"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> });</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>When providing a JSON object, Jazz will automatically create the CoValues for you.
To learn more about how permissions work in this case, refer to
<a href="/docs/react/permissions-and-sharing/cascading-permissions#ownership-on-implicit-covalue-creation">Ownership on implicit CoValue creation</a>.</p>
<h3 id="type-safety" class="group"><a href="#type-safety" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Type Safety</span></h3>
<p>CoMaps are fully typed in TypeScript, giving you autocomplete and error checking:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del="2 3"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">project</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.set</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"name"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Spring Vegetable Planting"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// ✓ Valid string</span></span>
<span class="line diff remove"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">project</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.set</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"startDate"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "2025-03-15"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// ✗ Type error: expected Date</span></span>
<span class="line diff remove"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Argument of type 'string' is not assignable to parameter of type 'Date'</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h3 id="soft-deletion" class="group"><a href="#soft-deletion" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Soft Deletion</span></h3>
<p>Implementing a soft deletion pattern by using a <code>deleted</code> flag allows you to maintain data for potential recovery and auditing.</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="3" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line diff add"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  deleted</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.optional</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.boolean</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">())</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>When an object needs to be &quot;deleted&quot;, instead of removing it from the system, the deleted flag is set to true. This gives us a property to omit it in the future.</p>
<h3 id="deleting-properties" class="group"><a href="#deleting-properties" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Deleting Properties</span></h3>
<p>You can delete properties from CoMaps:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">inventory</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.delete</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"basil"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Remove a key-value pair</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// For optional fields in struct-like CoMaps</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">project</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.set</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"coordinator"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> undefined</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Remove the reference</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h2 id="running-migrations-on-comaps" class="group"><a href="#running-migrations-on-comaps" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Running migrations on CoMaps</span></h2>
<p>Migrations are functions that run when a CoMap is loaded, allowing you to update existing data to match new schema versions. Use them when you need to modify the structure of CoMaps that already exist in your app. Unlike <a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/schemas/accounts-and-migrations#when-migrations-run">Account migrations</a>, CoMap migrations are not run when a CoMap is created.</p>
<p><strong>Note:</strong> Migrations are run synchronously and cannot be run asynchronously.</p>
<p>Here&#x27;s an example of a migration that adds the <code>priority</code> field to the <code>Task</code> CoMap:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Task</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> co</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">  .map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    done</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.boolean</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    text</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.plainText</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    version</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.literal</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">([</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">1</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 2</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">])</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    priority</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.enum</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">([</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"low"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "medium"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "high"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">])</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA"> // new field</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  })</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">  .withMigration</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">((task) </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=></span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">    if</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> (</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">task</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.version </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">===</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 1</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">      task</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.set</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"priority"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "medium"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">      // Upgrade the version so the migration won't run again</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">      task</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.set</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"version"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 2</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  });</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h3 id="migration-best-practices" class="group"><a href="#migration-best-practices" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Migration best practices</span></h3>
<p>Design your schema changes to be compatible with existing data:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Add, don&#x27;t change:</strong> Only add new fields; avoid renaming or changing types of existing fields</li>
<li><strong>Make new fields optional:</strong> This prevents errors when loading older data</li>
<li><strong>Use version fields:</strong> Track schema versions to run migrations only when needed</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="migration--reader-permissions" class="group"><a href="#migration--reader-permissions" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Migration &amp; reader permissions</span></h3>
<p>Migrations need write access to modify CoMaps. If some users only have read permissions, they can&#x27;t run migrations on those CoMaps.</p>
<p><strong>Forward-compatible schemas</strong> (where new fields are optional) handle this gracefully - users can still use the app even if migrations haven&#x27;t run.</p>
<p><strong>Non-compatible changes</strong> require handling both schema versions in your app code using discriminated unions.</p>
<p>When you can&#x27;t guarantee all users can run migrations, handle multiple schema versions explicitly:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> TaskV1</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  version</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.literal</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">1</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">)</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  done</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.boolean</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  text</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> TaskV2</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> co</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">  .map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">    // We need to be more strict about the version to make the</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">    // discriminated union work</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    version</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.literal</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">2</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">)</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    done</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.boolean</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    text</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    priority</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.enum</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">([</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"low"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "medium"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "high"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">])</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  })</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">  .withMigration</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">((task) </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=></span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">    if</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> (</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">task</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.version </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">===</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 1</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">      task</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.set</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"version"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 2</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">      task</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.set</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"priority"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "medium"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  });</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Export the discriminated union; because some users might</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// not be able to run the migration</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Task</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.discriminatedUnion</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"version"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> [TaskV1</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> TaskV2]);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> type</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Task</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> co</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">loaded</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">typeof</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> Task>;</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h2 id="best-practices" class="group"><a href="#best-practices" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Best Practices</span></h2>
<h3 id="structuring-data" class="group"><a href="#structuring-data" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Structuring Data</span></h3>
<ul>
<li>Use struct-like CoMaps for entities with fixed, known properties</li>
<li>Use record-like CoMaps for dynamic key-value collections</li>
<li>Group related properties into nested CoMaps for better organization</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="common-patterns" class="group"><a href="#common-patterns" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Common Patterns</span></h3>
<h4 id="helper-methods" class="group"><a href="#helper-methods" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Helper methods</span></h4>
<p>You should define helper methods of CoValue schemas separately, in standalone functions:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">import</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { co</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> z } </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">from</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "jazz-tools"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  startDate</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
