<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  endDate</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.optional</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">())</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">type</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> co</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">loaded</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">typeof</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> Project>;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> function</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> isProjectActive</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Project</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> now</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> new</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  return</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    now </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">>=</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> project</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.startDate </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">&#x26;&#x26;</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> (</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">!</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">project</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.endDate </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">||</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> now </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">&#x3C;=</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> project</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.endDate)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  );</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> function</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> formatProjectDuration</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  format</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "short"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> |</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "full"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> start</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> project</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">startDate</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.toLocaleDateString</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  if</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> (</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">!</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">project</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.endDate) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">    return</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> format </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">===</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "full"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> ?</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> `Started on </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">${</span><span style="color:#969696;--shiki-dark:#969696">start</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">}</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">, ongoing`</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> :</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> `From </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">${</span><span style="color:#969696;--shiki-dark:#969696">start</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">}</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">`</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> end</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> project</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">endDate</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.toLocaleDateString</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  return</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> format </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">===</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "full"</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">    ?</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> `From </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">${</span><span style="color:#969696;--shiki-dark:#969696">start</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">}</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> to </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">${</span><span style="color:#969696;--shiki-dark:#969696">end</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">}</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">    :</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> `</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">${</span><span style="color:#969696;--shiki-dark:#969696">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">project</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">endDate</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.getTime</span><span style="color:#969696;--shiki-dark:#969696">() </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">-</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> project</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">startDate</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.getTime</span><span style="color:#969696;--shiki-dark:#969696">()) </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">/</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 86400000</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">}</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> days`</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Project</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "My project"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  startDate</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> new</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"2025-04-01"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">)</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  endDate</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> new</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"2025-04-04"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">)</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">isProjectActive</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(project)); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// false</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">formatProjectDuration</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "short"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">)); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// "3 days"</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h4 id="uniqueness" class="group"><a href="#uniqueness" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Uniqueness</span></h4>
<p>CoMaps are typically created with a CoValue ID that acts as an opaque UUID, by which you can then load them. However, there are situations where it is preferable to load CoMaps using a custom identifier:</p>
<ul>
<li>The CoMaps have user-generated identifiers, such as a slug</li>
<li>The CoMaps have identifiers referring to equivalent data in an external system</li>
<li>The CoMaps have human-readable &amp; application-specific identifiers<!-- -->
<ul>
<li>If an application has CoValues used by every user, referring to it by a unique <em>well-known</em> name (eg, <code>&quot;my-global-comap&quot;</code>) can be more convenient than using a CoValue ID</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Consider a scenario where one wants to identify a CoMap using some unique identifier that isn&#x27;t the Jazz CoValue ID:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// This will not work as `learning-jazz` is not a CoValue ID</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> myTask</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> await</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Task</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.load</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"learning-jazz"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>To make it possible to use human-readable identifiers Jazz lets you to define a <code>unique</code> property on CoMaps.</p>
<p>Then the CoValue ID is deterministically derived from the <code>unique</code> property and the owner of the CoMap.</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Given the project owner, myTask will have always the same id</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">Task</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    text</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Let's learn some Jazz!"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    unique</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "learning-jazz"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    owner</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> project</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.owner</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA"> // Different owner, different id</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>Now you can use <code>CoMap.loadUnique</code> to easily load the CoMap using the human-readable identifier:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> learnJazzTask</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> await</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Task</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.loadUnique</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">  "learning-jazz"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">  project</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">owner</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.id</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>It&#x27;s also possible to combine the create+load operation using <code>CoMap.upsertUnique</code>:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">await</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Task</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.upsertUnique</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  value</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    text</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Let's learn some Jazz!"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  unique</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "learning-jazz"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  owner</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> project</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.owner</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p><strong>Caveats:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>The <code>unique</code> parameter acts as an <em>immutable</em> identifier - i.e. the same <code>unique</code> parameter in the same <code>Group</code> will always refer to the same CoValue.</p>
<ul>
<li>To make dynamic renaming possible, you can create an indirection where a stable CoMap identified by a specific value of <code>unique</code> is simply a pointer to another CoMap with a normal, dynamic CoValue ID. This pointer can then be updated as desired by users with the corresponding permissions.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>This way of introducing identifiers allows for very fast lookup of individual CoMaps by identifier, but it doesn&#x27;t let you enumerate all the CoMaps identified this way within a <code>Group</code>. If you also need enumeration, consider using a global <code>co.record()</code> that maps from identifier to a CoMap, which you then do lookups in (this requires at least a shallow load of the entire <code>co.record()</code>, but this should be fast for up to 10s of 1000s of entries)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="creating-set-like-collections" class="group"><a href="#creating-set-like-collections" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Creating Set-like Collections</span></h4>
<p>You can use CoRecords as a way to create set-like collections, by keying the CoRecord on the item&#x27;s CoValue ID. You can then use static <code>Object</code> methods to iterate over the CoRecord, effectively allowing you to treat it as a set.</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Chat</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  messages</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.list</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(Message)</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  participants</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.record</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> MyAppUser)</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> chat</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> await</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Chat</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.load</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(chatId</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  resolve</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    participants</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> true</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">let</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> participantList</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">[];</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Note that I don't need to load the map deeply to read and set keys</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">if</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> (</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">chat</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.$isLoaded) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">  chat</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">participants</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.set</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">me</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.id</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> me);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  participantList </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Object</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.keys</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">chat</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.participants);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">}</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>You can choose a loading strategy for the CoRecord. Use $each when you need all item properties to be immediately available. In general, it is enough to shallowly load a CoRecord to access its keys, and then load the values of those keys as needed (for example, by passing the keys as strings to a child component).</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { </span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">participants</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> } </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> await</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> chat</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.ensureLoaded</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  resolve</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    participants</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">      $each</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">        profile</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">          avatar</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> true</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">        }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">      }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> avatarList</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Object</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.values</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(participants)</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  (user) </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=></span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> user</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">profile</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.avatar</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div><div class="flex flex-row justify-start flex-wrap items-center gap-2
